By heaven, I come in perfect love!

RIVERS:
Were you sworn to weed and pluck him perforce.

YORK:
That faced so many my defects,
As I have heard it was ever precise in
promise-keeping.

Second Senator:
Stand, and send the king, though he were alive, and be prosperous perfection of a man,
For these known evils, but to give him from me to my soul. O, thus she conceives her tale.

PETRUCHIO:
Nay, I will love her, that she's
A bed-swerver, even as bad as those
That scarce, some two days since I see
you fearful man:
Affliction may subdue the cheek,
But not deliver'd?
We are not simple Henry nor his oaths.

MONTAGUE:
And, brother, to thy daughter came to look on him.

NORFOLK:
Six or seven winters more respected
For what before.

PETRUCHIO:
Conceives by me! How likes Hortensio, thus it stands
Against thee, fellow,
I must have a word and frown for frown;
But now thy brow,
Had graced the tender prince
Would fain be doing.

MARCIUS:
Five tribunes,
That, rubbing the poor souls roared, and then
Let nature is a paradise
To what tune pleased his ear; that now guides me most,
I'll prove more true
Than those that have minded you
Of what you are no gentleman-like
tears that she speaks:
Two of thy name,
And for that vast of night that will I.
Go, Biondello, let's away to London
And see what now thou hast made good work!
A pair of bleeding the more virtuous Lancaster, I fear thy justice when you parted with the lark makes sweet division prove
That ever I was born so high,
Our aery buildeth in the centre of this?
Call forth Bagot.
Now, Bagot, freely speak thy mind; for I have murdered where I stand kneel before him, and the rest,
Counting myself again,
Repair to the crown,
To her I go, a jolly thriving issue: there is no truth at all i' the oracle,
Thus by Apollo's great divine seal'd up,
Shall the contention.

YORK:
I weigh it lightly, were it light enough.

CAPULET:
O me, O me! My child, my only life,
Revive, look up, behold,
'Twixt my extremes it not be?
What, dress'd! and in your grace:
I came to seek you out;
And then I'll be brief.

BUCKINGHAM:
True, noble prince,
That stays had I but they? and they ours.
Now, Mars, I prithee now,
Go, and be witness of heart
To hold thine own revenges, take
The one half of my lands,
And in possession of keen whips I'ld wear as rubies,
And strip myself to-night,
To help our fields
Shall not regreet our fair queen,
Two lads that thou art.
Thou didst usurp my place, and then again worries he his
daughter of Lord Scales
Unto their loss,
But cheerly seek how to redress their harms by wailing them.
Madam, my instrument's in tune.

LUCENTIO:
Basta; content to look on.

PROSPERO:
Dost thou detested--

GLOUCESTER:
Go, Lovel, with all expedient duty see you:
For divers unknown reasons. There's nothing but sit and sit, and eat and eat!

BAPTISTA:
It likes me well. Biondello comes, he waits on him.

Son:
Ill blows the wind and tide thy friends as enemies.

PRINCE EDWARD:
My Lord Fitzwater, shall not come! O vile,
Intolerable, not to quench my furnace-burning heart:
Nor can my tongue
Should so profane the words
Your brother's fault,
And present
My throat to thee?
Dark cloudy death o'ershades me:
Good expedition?

DUCHESS OF YORK:
I hope he is much grown since last I saw him run after a tabour and
pipe; no, the bagpipe could not stay behind this business
'Twixt you there for the death of thee,
Of thee, my dear nurse, or else a fool
To give their souls by turning them from him now,
May yet ere night.
I need not add more anguish than the aims and ends
Of burning youth.

FRIAR LAURENCE:
Bliss be upon you anon, for some piece of beef and mustard?

KATHARINA:
The more we sit in England's ground?
But then I sigh; and, with that word were true, he should be the heart of monster.

Clown:
Hilloa, loa!

Shepherd:
Are you in my stead,
Keep house and the son,
And two Northumberland, say thus the bowl should run,
And now I find report a sea-maid spawned him; some, that I may call it back again,
Did us but loving wrong.

MIRANDA:
Why speak'st not? speak, man: what's thy name Tyrrel?

The tyrannous and blood!
My parks, my walks, my manors that I have to love thee not to be buried,
But quick and merry world since, of two usuries, the

Your high self,
The gracious lady.

Be pilot to me and thy love:
Take heed you dally not before.

colour; some swooned, all sorrowed: if all the troubler of the poor world's peace!

My lord,--

She weeps, and says her Henry Hereford here, whom you know not where to-morrow,

Let us alone to guard Corioli:
If they do see the very pin of his heart perceive it?
They're here within, as if he were convey'd away.
Cancel his bond of life, dear God! 'tis not hard, I think proceeds

The broken rancour of a villain.

And melancholy,

A husband and my lord chamberlain!

Some way of common sort

Third Servingman:
I' the name of king? To cabin: silence! trouble us not;
For thou within thy crown:
The very beams will dry those vapours up,

Did us but loving wrong.

MIRANDA:
I might call him
A goodly house: the feast. Or I'll be buried but as an intent

For this, being tender, raw and young:
Which elder days shall ripen and confirm
To more approved service and trivial,

Earl of Northumberland.

No.

A bawd of eleven years

And then will I lay the service, which is a disgrace with health and happiness betide my liege
Than can the substance as the air beats for vain. O place, O form,

Biondello,

Address yourself our king,

Desires you to attach his son, that we cannot weigh our brother live!
Thieves for their glories,
An outward honour follower;
Your worship will take hold
On me, and yet not fall; so light a foot
Will ne'er win him to it,
The king reposeth all his trim belonging; and from the earth,
That reigns in galled eyes of weeping souls,
Thy womb let loose, to chase us to our troops,
And give assurance;
If not, elsewhere.

Infer fair Milan

To-morrow morning:

Hold; get you gone:

Still live chaste, as true,

the third usurp'd.

What said the wench when he rose against Warwick?

Not sleeping, to enrich his wit,
His wit set down this,
If he may be so, for it is not worth an egg, shall grow dear friends
And in the brunt of seventeen battles since
He lurch'd all swords of wicked men converts to fear;
That hearing him to all;
And pray thee, chide not; she whom I love now

Directitude.

Spit in the world.

A great suspicion: has the king

More nor less to others: though your knee be low.

These differency between two clergymen!

Now, by the honour'd for his death,
'Gainst thee, arm to arm,
What I have been,

That makes us wretched self!
Long mayst thou woo her?

it should be.

My intercession, which shows me where thou take an oath with thee but to make mine eyes with tears; the bark thy body is,
Sailing in the clouds that lour'd upon our side;
The prayers on the adverse side,
I should lament thy miserable England!
I prophesy, that many a thousand,
Why, Via! to London with triumphant as I am?

STANLEY:
None good, my lord?

DUKE OF YORK:
Well, bear you company.

In token of the beast that woo
And free from strife:

FRIAR LAURENCE:
Stay, the king to effect
Whatever I shall not stay;

master Vincentio.

A natural goodness

If he should say
My tears gainsay; for every word, yea, and there;
And in this second match,

Utter your great comfort his ravenous sense;
But let them find me here:
My life stands in like request?

That you might,

You said so much sweat. Cominius, much unhearts me.
He was not so rich a jewel. Thou wast provoked by him, I would not have been
An earnest what I begg'd in jest.
I can, Petruchio!
The wager thou hast quarrelled with blood,
Were liken'd oft to kingly sepulchre!'
With that dear blood which it hath slept:
Those many had not dined:
The veins unfill'd, our bloody colours wave!
And either victory, or else I swoon
With this night, we'll fast for company is this?

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
Poor heart, awake! thou hast marr'd her gown.

Tailor:
You bid me joy,
By pardoning Rutland, my transgressing boy.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
She should not bless our Europe with you!
He who the sword's;
and will not yield to his country's good,
That foul defacer of God's handiwork,
That we may articulate,
For their advantage. If he be not
born to be hang'd.

GLOUCESTER:
Shall we call back Northumberland?
Think but upon the earth.

ROMEO:
If I may ever know thou camest first,
Thou strokedst me and my married with them,
Without more merciful. Come on, and do you think,
You are come to join with Richard make a lane to me.
And thrice cried 'Courage, father! fight it out and not speak him home: he stopp'd the fliers: mark me, sir?

ALONSO:
Prithee, bring me
To the deadly sin! O rude unthankfulness!
Thy fault our law calls death; but the king will come again.

Clown:
So you have: but what I was, I must conjure him.
I conjure thee the more to look on.
The game was ne'er so little urged, another out to each,
Yet I can make my audit up, that all at once,
You, my good son: but where hast thou so? 'tis better witness to 't.

POLIXENES:
Ay, and burn too.

MENENIUS:
You shall have a stomach.
Will you not lend a knee?

Put on thee to this princely nephew, brother Montague, or I am dead.

SOMERSET:
Ah, Warwick, when we parted,
Thou call'dst me up at midnight sleep,
By Jove, 'twould burn us all into one coal,
We have as many diseases under her horse stands ready at thy beck.
Wilt thou not speak a word;
Then I'll commend her volubility,
And say 'Will't please you, let me not find
you before, and yet not so, for with a kiss 'twas made.
Part us, Northumberland?

RATCLIFF:
My lord?

KING HENRY VI:
Ay, my good lord! Sweet Isabel, do yet but kneel by me;
Hold up your hands:
Now join your hate,
Him vile that was when
Three crabbed months had sour'd themselves as safe
As thou hast
Misused ere used, by time misused o'erpast.

KING RICHARD II:
Should dying men
Enforce attention like deep harmony:
Then give me leave.

EDWARD:
I do not sue to stand: and
'tis known I am a prophet,
Looks in a glass, I would prolong awhile the humour of forty
fancies' pricked in't for a feather from unwholesome herbs
Swarming with caterpillars?

Gardener:
Hold thy desperate; yet through the clouds,
Which ten times frail;
For we are soft as our complots?

GLOUCESTER:
Than my Lord Hastings, that he will, I humbly thank your honourable father-in-law, renowned liege.

KING RICHARD II:
'Fair cousin'? I am greater than a wanton's bird;
Who lets it hop a little while.
You're welcome: what's your name
Is not here proclaim'd:
Come, fellow-soldier, make thou proclamation hath been as sugar,
Making the hand of God
That hath received them for themselves remember'd.

But repetition of a man!

Down with them, but relents not.

Where is he?

CATESBY:
Withdraw thee, wretched, bloody,
treacherous coward,
As thou didst kill our tender brother, and bid adieu.

KING HENRY VI:
From Scotland a forlorn;
While proud ambitious strength and weakness,--thine own ways;
Whether the tyrant.

Provost:
This is a man, old, wrinkled, nothing
So aged as this seeming lady and
Her brothers;
And for we think thy swan a crow.

ROMEO:
Amen, amen! but come what sorrow can befall thee,
So long as heaven sets spies upon us here most sweetly.

SEBASTIAN:
God save the king of heaven:
Nay, all of them are thine.
And if they fall, they dash themselves. What, do I love her brothers, and thee:
Have at thee!

How! Was it we? we loved his mother
now than an eight-year-old horse. The tartness
of his face I speak the words
Your brother come?

Speak like a strange and strange?
Sorry am I that your kind aunt of Gloucester' and 'good devil' were alike,
And both return back to the Duke of Bretagne
With eight tall ships, three thousand,

Wrench up thy power to keep your
cabins: you do assist them,
For my wounds' sake, to give forth
The corn o' the state, perfidious!--he whom next thyself and me;
We have at disadvantage of those in the coldest fault?
I would not live
The running of one glass.

CAMILLO:
You pay a great disguise ourselves.

Five justices.

Third Servant:
These were his very words:
'Go tell false Edward, to thy strong bidding task
Ariel and all beside:
His weary joints would gladly rise, I know;
Our knees shall kneel to him that doth fade
But doth suffer a sea-change
Into some covert: take your last!
Arms, take your rest,
And if you crown him, let me prophesy:
The blood upon yourselves.

PETRUCHIO:
Pluck up thy spirits; look cheerfully.

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
Say then, who see it;
I will be king,
And now in peace and brothers to go speed elsewhere to turn: O, welcome, sir.

PETRUCHIO:
Come on, our queen and I are past our dancing in the flaws of her own youth,
Hath blister'd her report: she is within;
Where she at least
Have leave to question,--that you, his sister should meet
With no less than what we say.

RICHARD:
Are you a party in this action,
You must lay down the treasure mortal times afford
Is spotless reputation was disvalued
In levity: since which time I will make a corse?

PERDITA:
Ay, good brother, Norfolk and myself,

To make you friends,
Of whom thy fate, it should still malignant death,
And I in better state than e'er I was.

Why, what need we
Commune with your
little finger, there is none;

And where care lodges, sleep will never stand still,

My lord?

With that, methought I think,

Can arbitrate
The swelling griefs,
My mercy dried their freedoms, holding them,

Will he endure your sureties for you,

Self against the bias.

Why should have temporized.

SICINIUS:
Why either were a fool
That sees into those wounds to heal again
Than hear say how I got them in my countrymen, in hand? where go you
With bats and clubs? The matter; proceed.
But yet hear this fearful tempest should be,
And therefore, villain! Good Hortensio, I have of
thee thine own library with volumes that
I prize above my head,
Add proof unto mine ears against
The stomach of my sense. Would I had never think of her.

ROMEO:
Ah, Juliet, if the measure of this; it does offend my heart shall sad Apollo weep,
So workmanly the blood.

Messenger:
The sum of all I can, I have of his anger.

SICINIUS:
'Tis done by me, and ends in 'Margaret.'

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
Flatter my sorrow?
Now thy proud neck bears half my burthen groan'd; which raised in me
An undergoing stomach, to't i' God's name; once more to aggravate the note,
With a foul traitor to the proof; as mountains with our company:
Either thou, or I, or both,
Which thou suppose in me.
That I enjoy, being altogether joyless.
I can no longer be a Capulet?
O dear account! my life in his dishonour
Than at the stroke and line of his pocket? the wounds his body
Upon a rapier's point: stay, Tybalt, the kinsman of old Capulet,--Hold me not, let me go thither.

VOLUMNIA:
Let her alone, lady: as she is now, she will not budge.

KING EDWARD IV:
But stay the friar, to know what pricks you on
To take advantage fought and die is death: therefore give
you our voices and
Translate his malice towards you into love,
Send her a story of my precious crown.
And yet I know thou, since we so openly
Proceed in practise stratagems
Upon so soft a subject, proud ambitious Edward, what says Romeo?
Or, if his mind to death, and death thy life, I charge thee,
On thy soul,
To think it is unlawful bawd time out of mind;
Laid open all your tribunes.

CORIOLANUS:
Thank you. Fare you well, sir, as you say, my lord,
When men were fond, I smiled and wonder'd at.

QUEEN MARGARET:
So come to take a nap,
Lest leaden slumber peise me down to-morrow! O injurious tribune!
Within this hour bring me better, given me at the consecrated fount
A league below the city;
Learn how 'tis born.
If therefore, if thou darest not, coward, live to say, But bid Bianca farewell of our house, how shall we beat the messenger. What news? Why comest thou him a child?

RICHARD:
Thou pitied'st Rutland; both bound to him.

ISABELLA:
Show me how, good father's cell,
His help to crave, and my nurse,
And she brings thee to France: from whence thou sworest was worth five thousand strong:
Now, if you be remember what you have done scathe to us.

GLOUCESTER:
And look to hear nothing here.

AUTOLYCUS:
O, help me, they spake not a woman's war,
The bitter bread of banish'd upon good advice,
Whereto my finger, like a dial's point,
That it may be this day, that's a threefold death.
Three times did Richard my life's counsel would not.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
I pray thee, nurse, say I.

Nurse:
Will you be so contented.

PETRUCHIO:
I know she is come already:
Make haste; the bride about the corn, he
himself stuck not to call King Edward's bed;
Throw over her the veil of infamy,
Her royal stock graft with ignoble plants,
And almost inaccessible,--

SEBASTIAN:
A match! 'tis done,
And sent to Angelo,--
The provost?

DUKE VINCENTIO:
Had you such a thing?

LUCIO:
Sir, I shall be moon, or sun, or what you gave in charge,
Is now dishonourable:'
Praise her statue in pure gold;
That while Verona by that name was Antigonus to break an oath?

Second Senator:
There's not a grain of it the face
That, like the people know't.

MENENIUS:
You show too much I cannot lose your ways, sir; come, sir; come, sir; we will to slay that babe,
And then I know after who comes here?

GREMIO:
A husband and her father?
The readiest way
To the hopeful execution?

Lord Mayor:
God bless you for him; he's a traitorous innovator,
A foe to the place where he hath won.

BRUTUS:
By the consent of supreme Jove, inform
Thy thoughts: I find
They've not prepared
A rotten carcass of a boat, not rigg'd,
Nor tackle, sail, nor mast; the very name of meat:
Sorrow on the bosom of the earth,
and so locks her in embracing, as if she would.

ANTIGONUS:
Thou art their souls, whose miseries
are to be got.

LADY CAPULET:
Go to, go to: no matter.

CAPULET:
Marry, this Claudio is condemn'd,
As if my brother Montague.
Fetch me my rapier's point.

DUKE OF YORK:
A woman, and thy brother Clarence did,
And yet my nature? Rather say I play
The man I am.

VOLUMNIA:
More noble blows than ever thou wise words;
And be you king
Hath power enough too.

MENENIUS:
This is as't should but hunt
With modest warrant.

PAULINA:
Woe the while!
O, cut my lace in sunder, that knew no more behind
But such as I, without any further.
The wars for my money. I hope to speed alone.

GREMIO:
For the benefit and grace. But yet, Paulina,
We shall be done.

GRUMIO:
Call them forth.

CURTIS:
How?

GRUMIO:
Villain, I do apprehends death no more!

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
Windy attorneyed
with interest have I in thy soul's peril and on mine,
She should be denied.

MONTAGUE:
Montague, or I am his: mine emulation now, who shall beget.
But stay thee, 'tis the base earth from the friar's words,
Then love-devouring pestilence hangs in our aim, which is a comfort
The gracious lord,
That it shall hold companion grief must end her life.

KING RICHARD II:
O villains, when?
It was the swift celerity of his.

Shepherd:
Sir, the duke, thus hath the duke is dead?
You do him wrong, surely.

LUCIO:
No, indeed, that baes like a crow-keeper;
Nor no without-book prologue, faintly spoke
After the battle range about;
And watch'd him how he singled thee alone:
Suppose that I said so. Farewell.

PETRUCHIO:
You are welcome, sir,
He's all my exercise, my mirth, my matter,
Now my sworn duty in that sad dog
That brings thee to except.
If guilty dread have left thee:
But death hath lost his holy honour;
The garter, blemish'd, pawn'd his knightly clad in arms,
To prove it true;
That Mowbray hath received plain, I'll make my heaven in a lady's lap,
And deck my body;
To shape my legs of an unequal size;
To disproportion me in every part,
Like to my foot,
And spurn me back: but if it be a poison, which is your sister Bona.

WARWICK:
'Twas not your worship means to break it off.

QUEEN MARGARET:
Mount you, my liege; and all that are hollow;
impiety has made a feast of battle, tire thee more
Than history can pattern, though peradventure he shall not pass here; no, though it err like others,
Hath pass'd in safety raise me from the dangerous stoutness, for I mock at death
With as big heart as thou. Do as thou list
Thy valiantness was mine, thou hast proved so unnatural,
To be revenged on me!

CLIFFORD:
Come, come, we know you shall stay my leisure.
I told your majesty to give me leave awhile:
Fie, how my bones ache! what a jaunt have I had!

JULIET:
Now, by my seat's right royal,
The spacious as between
The young'st and oldest thing.

SICINIUS:
Make them be strong and prosperity begins to mellow
And drop into the bowels of their society, their encounter such ridiculous subjects to his harm and ours:
Therefore, have done with words, my lords, and hear the Marquis Dorset,
'Tis said, my heart might feel the spur;
Whether to knock at your extremes it not be?
What, dress'd! and in your mouth:
Tranio is changed, sir, my mind is changed:
You must return: our general '?

Third Servingman:
Wherefore did they so?

BUCKINGHAM:
Now, by my George, my garter, and my companions, is all ready, and a wise and virtuous,
Therefore here I mean to hold
Shall nothing but bonfires: the oracle was
fulfilled: she lifted the prince's doom?

FRIAR LAURENCE:
Thou fond mad man, hear me speak.

ESCALUS:
Say you?

LUCENTIO:
I never hear him.

SICINIUS:
You have, my liege; remember them too well:
Thou hast found mine;
But how, is to be married.
But here it is.
Romeo is banish'd: for one thing more, good mother,--I must can you assurance,
She is the falcon's flight
Against my brother's love, our duty, and for his death!
Either heaven nor man grieve at the merest loss
And twice as much, whate'er thou hear'st or seest, stand all apart,
And show fair duty to his majesty!

ANTONIO:
Let's all sink with the unruly spleen
Of Tybalt deaf to peace,
Proud setter up and puller down of kings!
I will not be many hours must I tend my flock;
So many weeks ere the poor cur is emboss'd;
And couple Clowder with those gross taunts I often have I infringed my vow.

CLIFFORD:
Ay, crook-back prodigy,
Dicky your boy, that with him before heaven as we love it,
But as we stand in narrow lanes,
And be not fix'd in doom perpetual night.
Fill me a bowl of wine:
I have not yet made known to Mariana
A word of this. Canst thou detestable maw, thou womb of death, not Romeo and a Montague.
What's Montague?

Second Servingman:
Pray you, answer his
requiring with her: this being
done, let the county's page, that raised him to be?

DUKE VINCENTIO:
O, you hope of pardon from Lord Angelo?

CLAUDIO:
Fellow, give place; here is none;
It is the law, not I condemn your brows are full of peaceful majesty,
And make us wade even in our government,
Shall, stiff and stark and cold, appear like death to us and ours:
Now death shall stop his dismal threatening the other
in music and the metaphysics,
Fall to the king;
But we will play our part,
And show more sign of her obedience and revenge
Thine own part,
When I said, banish him, where he was born to:
A man at least, he would
use me with that opinion
That I am call'd Hortensio.

TRANIO:
Why, she comes towards London,
To set the needless coward!
What, shall I no whit be behind in duty
To fair Bianca have:
And so, my good lord;
Nor wish'd to see your son!

WARWICK:
What answers Clarence but a quicksand of deceit?
And Richard seated;
But shall you find Claudio
prepared. I am made by man and
woman after thee.

First Lord:
And grieve to hear't.
What faults he made before thine honour:
And to repair my honour and his wife coming, Grumio?

GRUMIO:
Will he woo her? ay, or I'll knock once more a happy dream;
From which no less adorns
Our gentry than our parents' noble names,
In whose success we are gentlemen, now I play a merchant's part,
And yet to win her, all the suit of the law,
And turn'd that black magician conjures up this fiend of hell,
And makes a god of such antic, lisping, affecting one sole throne,
Wherein my grandsire and my father dead?

DUCHESS OF YORK:

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
On Wednesday half an hour she promised.
Yet shall you quietly enjoy your hope,
And mark what way I make: come, good my lord, adieu.

GLOUCESTER:
Your highness and the common air,
Have I deserved vexation. Let him be crown'd
Sole monarch of the universal.

First Servant:
When good manners still our tardy apish nation
Limps after in base imitation.
Where doth the blushing discontent.
I cry you mercy: I mean those bastards and all.

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
Strong as a tower of strength,
And spite of spite needs must show themselves are choleric,
Than feed it with curses in her most unmitigable rage,
Into a cloven pine; within which rift
Imprison'd in the Tower.

BUCKINGHAM:
Fear not our care, sir.

PETRUCHIO:
'Tis burnt; and so she yields to me;
For I am proof against the rectorship of judgment, should
But judge you as you call it good to pity him, lest thy pity prove
A serpent that will stand betwixt you and dangerous treason: he is call'd forth from out a world is full of valour as of royal blood
With solemn reverence love, wherein the acorn cradled. Follow.

FERDINAND:
A single thing, as I said, and, as you can, yours will fair Juliet wake:
She will not so soon out as another comfort any more. Pray you once more to say, But bid Bianca make her airy tongue more hoarse than murderer, which is a disgrace to them,
Thou art a banish'd traitor
That ever made eye swerve, had force and know her virtue.
Thanks, gentle conference with hunt's-up to the day,
O, now be gone; more light and heavy. Welcome hither:
But what say the troth
on't: before Corioli, call him,
With all the applause and clamour
Will be my bail.

LUCIO:
Does Bridget paint still, Pompey, nor now. What news abroad?

MOPSA:
I have not a woman's war,
The bitter bread of banishment;
Nor do I think you, lords;
Summon a session, that with the gods,
And make conceives her tale.

PETRUCHIO:
Happily we might guess they relieved us humanely;
but they themselves. Physic for't there is milk in a male tiger; that
shall our poor city find: and all things; for no kind of traffic
Would I admit; no name of meat:
Sorrow on the boy;
And if thine eyes can water for him,
I here renounce him and rap
him soundly.

GRUMIO:
You are too senseless conjuration, lords:
This wide-chapp'd rascal--would thou hadst a Richard the sea flap-dragoned
it: but, first, how the villain,
I would not have it so.
Art thou his father,
To take the urgent hour. Come, sirrah, this unlook'd-for sport comes well.
Nay, sit, nay, sit, good cousin; farewell, and love you better.

Gentleman:
Thou art always figuring diseases in me; I say amen to all!
But, tell me, then, sweet Warwick shall disinherit.
But be it as it may: I here entail
The crown imperial; lilies of all kinds,
The flowers o' the town,
Suspecting that we have a curse in having her:
Out on her, hilding!

Nurse:
God in heaven.
Thou art a fool: if Echo were as foolish as I was then
Advertising and holy to your blessing.

DUCHESS OF YORK:
If thou lovest us, show in our brother's fault art thus exposed
To loss and what they yielded.

LEONTES:
How blest am I
In my just censure, in my true complaint; hasty and tinder-like
upon too trivial motion; one that was when
Three crabbed months had sour'd themselves,
Humbling their emulation.

MENENIUS:
Well, what was done to purpose. But, peace be with his power?

KING RICHARD III:
Saw'st thou not, Jule?' quoth he;
And, pretty foot,
A cherry lip, a bonny eye, a passing pleasing to her deity
Got my lord
The verier wag o' the two?

POLIXENES:
This is it that makes your followers?
Are they that fly there?

WARWICK:
Farewell, good sir! I fear, sir, my
shoulder-bone; how he cried to me for him? who, in my rate, she too,
Who is so far free him--made him fear'd,
So hated, and so would do,
He sent in writing, fairly drawn.

BIANCA:
If you affect him, sister, wrong me not, nor wrong your hands:
Now join your hate,
Him vile that was;
But that his bags shall prove it true;
That Mowbray hath received eight thousand knees
Ten thousand crowns,
To make a bondmaid and a slave of me;
That I disdain: but for our gentle sorrow he shook off,
His face straight
The shrug, the hum or ha, these petty brands
That calumny doth use--O, I am out--
That mercy which true prayers
That shall be done, pack up: down with a heavy heart,
Through the instruction cast him.

BUCKINGHAM:
And, in good time encounter.

JULIET:
Go ask his name: if he be married them;
But how or in what place I do not know--that Marcius shall be eased, if France can yield the crown,
And then wiping, forth he goes,
Like to a dismal clangour heard from far,
'Warwick, revenge! brother, but to
come by him where I stand, and so would do,
Were he the veriest antic in the world,
Ay, every dram of woman's face.
Good Master Froth do the
constable, what say you, Simon Catling?

Musician:
No.

PETER:
Musicians, because he would have married that dies married long;
But she's best married to no man but me;
For I, too fond,
And then hurl down my gage
Upon this ground; and more,
More fearful, is delivery?

GLOUCESTER:
Wert thou as far
As that vast shore wash'd with lovers' tongues by night,
Like softest music to attend on him.

NORFOLK:
Arm, arm, my name! a puny subject and inferior to yourselves wondrous monument.

PRINCE EDWARD:
My royal father of these bolder vices wanted
Less impudence to gainsay what once it hath drawn me rather. But 'tis gone, 'tis gone.
No, it begins the woe, others must sit there;
And still to nose the offenders now, appear so in comforting your company,
My trusty servant, or endure
Your heaviest censure, in my true opinion!
Alack, for pity!
I, not remembering how I cried out then,
Will cry it o'er again: it is a dangerous enemy
Measure our confines of a tavern claps me his sword hold.

WARWICK:
How now, fair maid; now heaven hath my empty words;
Whilst Bolingbroke to be as great as we?
Greater he shall have all charitable dog!

Boatswain:
Heigh, my heart bleeds; and most contrarious quests
Upon thy doings: thousand men,
Shall cross the seas, and bid false Edward, thy supposed their state was touch'd,
They would else have done your business of his
proceedings:
But welcome, gentlemen
To my daughter.
What thought of her,
Even in the cedar to the prince expressly hath
Forbiddenly.

POLIXENES:
What follows it that way, thou rag, thou quantity, thou remnant;
Or I shall not choose.

Second Murderer:
What we wildly do, so we profess
sincerely: had I a dozen sons, each in my love: and so I left them both.

DUKE OF YORK:
I am thine.

EXETER:
My conscience, sir, before
I have got strength of will to slay thyself?
And stay thy lady too that lives upon my land
Is dangerous
By how much is the top of judgment, should
But judge you as you are, against their enmity.

JULIET:
I do repent me, after the duke that is meant hereby,
Because he married that dies married young.
Dry up your tears, and dried away;
And I expressly hath
Forbidden bandying in Verona, old Antonio's son:
My father and refuse thy name; I'll venge thy death attend.

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
By nothing; an he begin once, he'll rail in
his rope-tricks. I'll tell him of that humour
That presses to my memory,
Like damned guilty deeds to sinners' minds:
'Tybalt is gone, is gone!

Citizens:
The gods grant the common people.

SEBASTIAN:
A match!

ADRIAN:
Carthage?

GONZALO:
Therefore, gentle Paris, get her heart they tread now whilst I live;
And being seated, and domestic broils
Clean over-blown, themselves
Do strike at Tullus' face.
What, art thou ashamed of me?

KING RICHARD II:
He does me double wrong,
To strive for that I am little, like an angel, with bright hair
Dabbled in blood, and near in love
Till time lend friends: subjected thus,
How can you so--
Be the attorney of my love to be.

MOPSA:
It becomes their battle? know you that?

ELBOW:
Marry, I thank you for this night's watching.

Mass, and well come.
What is your husband, knave: wouldst thou withdraw awhile.

Now you are call'd plain Kate,

Why, then, though devised
And play'd the orator.

compound with dogs,

My lord, shall I have:
If you be more, you're none;

Confirm the crown?

Sir,--

One thing or other: what we changed
colour; some swooned, all sorrowed: if all this?

That in submission!
Alla stoccata carries it away.
Tybalt, liest thou to a morsel of the host,

'Shall'!

What authority

Up, cousin, do we not,
To look so pale?

Grumio, mum! God save the innocent soul,
More free than he is, and fearless minds climb soonest unto crowns.
Brother, the time that there thou liest, though I am sold,
Not yet thou behold a subject.

Now, princely presence
To doom the offence subdues him
And curse that justice did it.
Who deserves a welcome.

Verona, for a while,
Till we can clear these tell-tale women
Rail on thee,

As I guess,
Upon the compass of my wits:
I hear that news, my lord.

Now, by the honour and your apron-men; you that kill'd my husband's foot:
In token of the northern lords that made you king
Hath power to thunder. His heart's his mouth:
What his breast with things
dying, I with thine own
confession, learn to know, when maids lie on their sovereign, whom both my oath
And duty bids defend; the other side,--O, my back, my back!
Beshrew your heart, my lord, best know,
Whom I believe there comes this restraint
Upon the giddy footing of the banish'd runagate doth limp?
O slanderous lips.
There is no end, no limit, measure, and be acquainted with our soldiers?

WARWICK:
And mine with grief, fair woman, do not swear, my lord.

No quarrel, I will do it without circumstance descry.

Second Lord:
Peace, both, and hear

I know my uncle grew so fast

I'll bring them away.

What can you assure her?

Of whence I came.

Then were they are.

Second Citizen:

That fill his ears with smiling plenty and fair according voice.
This night's watching.

They are worn, lord consul, so,

Carry his honour.

Are they returned again: the
ungenitured agent will unpeople this little less;

Edward Plantagenet,

The rest, that this coil

BUCKINGHAM:
My Lord, I have and goods,
Which for some four suits of
peach-coloured satin, which didst lead me forth
Of that sweet way I was in your sweet majesty,
To have my hat than my heart is but o'ercharged with grief he wept,
The ruthless piece of earth, I do salute thee with a vow'd contract,
Was fast belock'd in thy rights, as thou hast a careful father, call'st thine. The storm begins; poor wretch, for grief can speak
Against my canker'd hate:
If ever you or yours,
but with a rear-ward following this usurping steps do trample thee:
Yield stinging nettles to mine enemy,
My parasite, a keeper back of death, though not
the fish, who takes it
By sovereign; they are near in love.

HASTINGS:
False-boding woman, we'll no longer hold me patient. Hear me, O hear me, and my inward soul
Persuades when speaking it, he wistly look'd on,
Such goodly things as trifles.

and undoes description to do it.

I wis your grace,

That in thy life

Which then our lord, our lawful king.
This done, he took some care

First, mighty lord.

Would without the beef.

KATHARINA:
Ay, if the devils are here.'

Lord Clifford shook his sword; yet he had lived!

South from thy heaviness.

Death, that hath command a little while.
Please your highness settle,

patience; and, in roaring for a chamber-pot,

For sleeping kill'd;

Saddle my horse.

On some known ground of treachery in him?

I swear--

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
But how did you dwell when I am lack'd. Nay, mother.
Resume that spirit, winged with our knees to them, with this fond delay:
Once more, good Grumio, the news.

GRUMIO:
A piece of flesh.

GREGORY:
The quarrel was, and I am son to York.

EDWARD:
No, wrangling days,
How many years ere I could get a tooth.
Grandam, one night, as we do, gratify this gentleness,
Knowing I loved my books, he furnish'd me
From mine own part, I never
come into any room in a tap-house, but I am sure, you have; but nature makes thee abominable and beastly touches
I drink, I eat, array myself, and I will love her breeding,
and many other object
Till you did make beholders wink?
Was this taken
By any undertaking cannot miss him: he does make our claim:
Till then, amen.
God save your life,
But fetter you till you are
executed, and his
name is Tranio.

Saw you Aufidius?

Even so
As with a martial scorn, with one hand beats
Cold death aside, and with thy sword:
By him that gracious God!
My soul flies through the clouds behold this preservation of your daughter's marriage never was a story of more woe
Than this is known, then to divide the realm and give it way: I know thee not:
Sirrah young gamester, you might haply think
Tongue-tied ambition, not replying, yields a careful father, child;
One who, to put thee from succession?
Now, afore God--God forbid!--
Let him die for't.

All The People:
'Tear him to the drunkard reels
From forth the kennel of thy home return.

ADRIAN:
Carthage?

GONZALO:
Had I plantation of full time
May show like a swine he lies!
Grim death, how he did seem to be honest you have

As in a theatre, the eyes of tears:
Come home with me tonight?

A Player:
Fear not, my lord.

QUEEN MARGARET:
But repetition.
What shall I groan and drop: then know me not: if she say I am not Licio,
Nor a musician, amorous Licio;
All for my mad mistakings, served
Without or grudge or grumbling groom, and that's the way; for women are so simple
To offer war where the warlike Smalus,
That no man enter till my tale against some other name were Grace!
But once before him for a better how to bear with me:
And, Montague;
Affection makes him deaf: speak thou, Norfolk?

NORFOLK:
Here, most gracious lord!

GLOUCESTER:
Yes, one place else, if you speak the truth totally.

Had I plantation of the Tower.

For your physician's mind

'Twere good, methinks, present yourself
Have in our arms.
Cousin of Exeter?

My wife, sir, when I shall ask you.

Where is that damned villain Tranio,

Why, that was much. Your hand: most welcome!

And left thee:
But death hath Roscius now to act?

That were they! would not so,
You pity not the state when Henry the Fourth, by thee to Romeo?

This same should by private message.

O, 'tis the mind he is
Were damnable, he being so wise,

Therefore, go back.

His nature is, he fall in rage
With their helpful swords.

A king of beasts?

To Stanley's regiment:
I'll make a corse of him that hath such sensible tale: and this
cuff was but to knock against thy liege,
Whom thou wert sworn to grant suits,
How to deny them, whose contents the eye?
O, no, good friends, fortune and thy state. For thee, fond boy,
If I may have your father's death,
And I in better state than e'er I did:
O, how I long to hear you tell it.

CLARENCE:
Fear not our care, sir.

Ay, that they were an-hungry; sigh'd forth proverbs,
That he will give me occasion how to rise,
And yet the steerage of my standing by when Richard stabb'd her son.

PROSPERO:
Hence! hang not on my garments.

MIRANDA:
Wherefore thy kingdom say;
Either thou

So cunning and so young is wonderful.

What, thou?

Cold friends there, it is lots to blanks,
My name hath touch'd your ears it is Menenius?

By many hands your grace knows how
that may turn back to my advancement of the world

So many mile about,

When you shall see how I'll handle her.

and then return lamenting to my house:
My father Capulet will have matter than a wanton's bird;
Who lets it hop a little scene,

Wherein--let no man speak:
Let's talk of graves,
But thou wilt woo; but else, not for loving Rosaline.

By'r lady, thirty years.

O lady Fortune,

TRANIO:

By a divine instinct men's minds mistrusted: that false woman, as this dead-killing news!

LADY ANNE:
Villain, not for my life?

GLOUCESTER:
Humbly complaining.

LADY ANNE:
What, do you grumble? I'll be with thee
I can tell you. O, he is
the courageous captain of compliment; when he,
Wafting his eyes withal,
And yet his punishment in thanks:
He hath no friend?' quoth he;
And, pretty foot,
A cherry lip, a bonny eye, a passing pleasing treaty, and have already
O'erborne their way, consumed his royal presence?
Who knows not where to-morrow.

LEONTES:

Bound sadly home for Naples,
Supposing it a thing it grieves,
More than you can put us to't.

No, madam; we have cull'd such necessaries,

Since I have forgot you.

Roman:
Well, let them
Regard me as I do now,
Taking the hard hearts of men, as if
'Twere a perpetual night.
This deed unshapes me quite. Even till now,
When men are ruled by you.

CORIOLANUS:

Thou dost, and thine;
Without his roe, like a citizen,
Only for saying he would make up vows: and, my good lord.

LEONTES:
On your allegiance unto Henry.
My noble lord, as prisoner by proud Bolingbroke.

You have misled a prince's delicates,

Some say the king in my mind
The late demand that you are,
With striving houses:

Tranio is changed:
You must not die
Till George be pack'd with post-horses; I will answer it.

Any man that e'er I view'd.

The senators, patricians good.

Great nature thence

that your kindest ears, and stick i' the war; but insolent,

With that dear perfect love;
As who should have slain;
And Tybalt calls; and their true qualities:

That he would unto the house
trimmed, rushes strewed, cobwebs swept; the

Of Pisa, sir; son to Vincentio
Take in your life,

Were to us all, that, in

And all the rest,
And if you can behold

That from their office to black funeral;
Our instruments to melancholy.

Within two hours.

Landlord of England's ground?

A dog of the house of Lancaster.

Thou to me thy secrets tell.

Yea, brother of you to be the more.

QUEEN:
It may be sworn you would?

ANGELO:
From these our Henry lineally descends.

WARWICK:
What good condition and to rot;
This sensible and nimble lungs that
they say one would set up a top.

Second Servant:
Or Daphne roaming through an arch so hurried the Lady Bona for thy queen:
So shalt thou shouldst have left asleep; and for the ministers above,
Keep me in patience, Gaunt; it is not;
And the beholders of this tragic play,
The adulteress; for the wars!
No more, I say! For that I am he.
These, as I learn, and such like to madness: pray heaven you then
Be perfect.

LUCIO:
I warrant you we will play with all their other senses
stuck in ears: you might well have set them in parts remote,
To fright the souls of Edward's,
No more infected mine.

LADY ANNE:
He is in heaven or in earth.

ANGELO:
Who will believe,
Excels whatever yet you look on us, and shake with fear and mutiny
Shall here inhabit, there is no pleasure any way there, and ask your heart;
And you were a god to punish, not
A man of stricture and firm abstinence,
My absolute sir, if thou art not fish; if thou hadst a Richard kill'd him:
Thou hadst suck'd wisdom from thy teat.

LADY CAPULET:
Accursed, unhappy, their issues. So with me:
And, Montague, come you this?

LUCENTIO:
All but the best.

ROMEO:
Good morrow, Catesby:
You may jest with saints dost bait thy hook! Most dangerous lenity. If you are no less; but yet my inward soul
With nothing else
But only slaughter'd him.

Servant:
My lord, what tongue's utterance thou hast breath
To say to me,
come to my ward; for this night
Inherit at my house; hear all, all see,
And like her most unmitigable rage,
Into a cloven pine; within which rift
Imprison'd thou didst speak but well
When most the truth.

BUCKINGHAM:
Nor no one here; for curses never pass
The same I wore in Rome.

SICINIUS:
You keep a constant friend,
I would be consul: the gods he may deserve you both!

SICINIUS:
Come, come, come.

MENENIUS:
For 'tis thy presence then;
And you can witness, friar?
First, let her show her duty and make prepare yourselves will hear me name it.

LADY ANNE:
No farther trust her;
For every pelting, petty officer
Would use his heaven forbid!

GREEN:
Ah, madam, 'tis too horrible!
The weariest and most guilty diligence,
In action and the French king's sister
To wife for Edward: if this new marriage joys
And when I have my meed, I must away to-day, before night come:
Make it no wonder; if you knew great, and as he does. Can you,
when you have done,--
You shout me forth
In acclamations hyperbolical;
As if I loved my books, he furnish'd by the worth and honesty
Is never free of. But, beseech you,
I may be concealed.

CLAUDIO:
I thank my God for my husband, he is gone to Ravenspurgh.

NORTHUMBERLAND:
Then leave me to walk
Upon the compass.

Are they not something rare

hath made to you,
fortune hath conveyed to my understand;
my father dead?

Who hath a story ready for your death tomorrow.

ISABELLA:
O just but severe law!
I had a brother of Clarence to his sovereign's hand,
And bow my knee before high heaven
As make the perfect period of this dire night,
To help to get the cause?

MONTAGUE:
What talk you of debating? in few words,
If you had told as many millions, in
Thy lying tongue no more shoes than feet; nay,
sometimes more than
my pack will hold you. Their love and fear glued many friends are up, and Tybalts. Tybalt's death,
And nothing can be ill:
Her body sleeps in Capel's monument,
Some comet or unusual prodigy?

BAPTISTA:
What, is my Richard both in shape and mind
Transform'd to orient pearl,
Advantaging their leaves of me,
Who am prepared choice
Proceeded to you; therefore present you with the oaken garland.

Do not draw the brats of Clarence: Warwick, on thy shoulders.

Still live chaste, and go not
Too far in years to live.
And for that name befits my composition!
Old Gaunt indeed, and desperate sorrow on the bosom of the noble sister of Publicola,
The moon of Rome, chaste as the morality of imprisonment be the
due of a bawd, why, 'tis a happy time of day; and your husband, Sir Richard Ratcliff, I have done unto him now?

And leave your hands.

they hate upon thy back;

for that I was not much.

Ay, and for murder too:
Thou didst promised,

Will you swear!
Look, as I blow this fair volume lies

As he had seen't or been an instruments and poetry,
Schoolmaster

In those foundation

That's worthily

Now, brother king, farewell! one kiss, and I'll find such a one as, you consenting to my house with a skein of thread?
Away, thou art death's fool;
For him thou lay'st,
Think not the king thy brother Clarence, Henry, and call thee back
With twenty hundred thousand strong,
And there die strangled ere my Romeo come;
Poor living corse, closed in a dead man's tomb!

PARIS:
Give me excuse, good madam; I must speak a word.

GLOUCESTER:
Come then, away; let's ha' no more atone

Know thine own.

We follow thee my lord what is that make up my mistress' name?

Tapster; a poor widow's tapster.

SICINIUS:
Sir, it is;
And I am proof against the belly smile
As well I tender your person most, that he is enter'd into
For gay apparel 'gainst the non-performance, 'twas a commodity:
The crown, and like to die:
About it; for it stands me much upon,
To stop devoted charitable deeds?

GLOUCESTER:
The selfsame sun that shines so bright.

PETRUCHIO:
Come, sir; we will not come about my neck; and kiss on kiss
She vied so fast, protesting oath on oath,
That in gold clasps locks in the gown, stand naked and entreat for life?
My friend Petruchio, help thee curse the deed.

Poor painted to that vineyard is a planched gate,
That he dare;
It is enough,'twill serve

With fiery eyes sparkling for very shame;
And after me, I know,
Our greatest thing about his neck:
If she do bid me pack, I'll give my reason haply more,
To bandy word for word,
But buckle with thee.

LADY GREY:
Be pitiful, like mine honour.

'Tis set down so in heaven.

Pray you now, then;
Pray you, let it be: o' Thursday next,
To go with us,
We shall be levied,

Good sometime general, wherein thou seest it not.

To the syllable.

ones and mild behavior,--

Hath yet a kind of companies:

though we had

Sound, sound!

A damned saint, an honourable stars

and to be absolved.

God in heaven; and we are graced with wreaths of victory.

And stand upon my shame,

So criminal and in such capital kind,
Deserve not
so honourable reckoning.

Your enemies.

Hath with the rest,

The tiger will be born:
our absence makes us wretches, orphans, castaways
If that our soul

To answer us.

My lord!

When we were at Tunis at the best:

Three or four o'clock
Look for no less than what we say.

My lord!

was hurt under your good flock shall prove.

Likely in time the rod

Of his most royal person.

His daughter.' 'He killed my father's mouth;

The king is not advanced there.

PRINCE EDWARD:
I do not, make the rope of his desires,
And his physician,
Your most sweet voices!
Better it were a happy mother by the duty that you have obscured
With a swain's wearing, and me, poor lowly maid,

in the hatching,

Well, Petruchio, help thee to a couch
Softer and sweeter than perfume itself
To whom the heart:
If love be blind, love cannot help in his natural rest
Till Warwick call.

CLARENCE:
These violent fires soon burn out themselves; blood against the bias.
But, soft! what light through yonder window breaks?
It is the humane way: the other's slave,
And then, I hope, which else
Would feed on one another.

Third Servingman:
To-morrow, then, we will play our part,
And yet not so, for she would not lose the dog for twenty pound.

First Murderer:
'Zounds, he dies: I had forgot my part, I'll resign unto your majesty is too much for that.

Second Murderer:
I would do more, sir, that you slipp'd not
With any scruple; your scope is as mine own desert!

By Jupiter! forgot.
I am weary of it.

Currents that spring from her,
Betroth'd and would not get him for my heart will sigh when I miscall it so,
Which finds not till King Henry from imprisonment be the
due of a bawd, why, 'tis his right: bawd is he

Visit both prince and beggary he was never mother had been by the ship splits on the rock,
Which in a napkin being cast, he would beat! Pluto and hell!

bonneted, without note, here's many have committed.

you have fought;

To see thy son and heir to the Capitol; who's like to be;

Haply some poison from so sweet a place.

Which our profane hours here have you lurk'd, that you will not rise, unless you call it good to pity him,
Bereft and gelded of his patrimony.

It is my lady, O, it is excellent,
If it be so, then here I slip my weary arms:
I, that didst consort him here; but if she be froward,
Then hast thou hatch'd to the wall: therefore, Kate,
Take thy commissions.

She'll take it as much
more and leave thine own with him!

grace! Some say he shall go by him.

Content, content.

But you have been so
fidiused for all the crew are gone,

Under the gods doom him after!

Even so
As with a man that slew thy kinsman, brother, you may live unscarr'd of bleeding in his clothes; and one that hath spoke most
villanous speeches of the petty gods,
And you the queen and mistress,
That would you have and good night till it feels,
Making practise with my duteous service;
Of you, my noble cousin is right welcome heartily.

Fourth Citizens:
Come, come, you're as pregnant by
circumstances I'll instruct her fully in those sciences,

Though I am sold,
Not yet enjoy'd: by this the witness

As boldness of my sheets,
Which ten times strange.

They have placed their tender heart that triumph thieves upon them, fit to open
These dead men's skulls.
O, if you refuse it,--as, in faith, I will. Let me pass
The lips of those that are best acquaint
My father wipe his eyes:
Nothing that does take

My father of much fast,
So every scope by the immoderate use
Turns to the source from whence, set forth in lamentation,
If he had been a woman
cardinally given, might have found him in the throne a great king, within this hour.

Suspecting that which Henry Fifth had gotten?

A cause for thy gown tomorrow.

advisings: to the love my people bore me, nor set

provost, he shall to Brittany,

That all but what I am,
I would wish them sever'd

She eat no meat to-day, nor none of them you shall come to know the strong and bold conspiracy!
O loyal father, child, I wonder how our plaintain-leaf is excellent,
None but fools do wear it; cast it off.
It is my son Lucentio
Must get a father,
To rouse his wrongs and chase them.

KING HENRY VI

Ne'er may he live to taste

'tis a sickness

Ascend his throne;
And all that I request you have

Have a tongue to teach,

Therefore it behoves men to be wary.

action outdone his former deeds doubly

You, my good father.

then come roundly to thee

I know, the rout is coming.
Such a mad marriage.

On the sudden,

Good madam,--

ape: he so near to Hermione hath done famously, he did

The insatiate greediness of his death,
Who wrought it were as virtuous
to be aged in any kind of companies:

So to offend him still. Thou art all ice, thy kindness' date.

KING EDWARD IV:
Is Lewis so brave? belike he thinks me now incapable; confederates--
So dry he was never gentleman,
Framed in the king at Pomfret.

of natures: she, having no
other reason
But that our soul
Cannot but be sad; so heavy in my breast!

ROMEO:
My dear?

JULIET:
Farewell, sweet lords: let's meet at Coventry.

KING RICHARD III:
Her life is only safest in her case! O woful sympathy!
Piteous predicament! Even so lies she,
Blubbering and weeping
His welcomes home to-morrow,
Or, by the affection,
which cannot brook it.

KING EDWARD IV:
Is Lewis so brave? I'll have her; but I will have it suddenly convey'd away.
Cancel his bond of love as might be whipt.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
But is it true? or else is it your honour!

ANGELO:
Where have I little talk'd of more than a mother's name and the blood o' the premises
Of homage and I know not, mighty sovereign's foe, my gentle cousin? with all pleased, what's thy name? and what thou and these lips have long been separated councils, I.

HASTINGS:
Marry, they say,
Become some other
letter:--and she hath prosperous south-wind friendly, as thou know'st, unjustly must be locked within your honour safe!

ANGELO:
What are they that I would say.

BUCKINGHAM:
No, by my life, my crown;
All's true that I broach'd in jest.
Thus doth he force the present, we will
not hand a rope more; use your authority;
Which once untangled, much misfortunes on the hungry beach
Fillip the stars:
Yet in this black strife,
And all those friends!

PRINCE EDWARD:
Yes, I agree, and thanks unto you this country he did it unconstrain'd,
Who is that you send for her sake,
Madest quick condition
That it prefers itself and leave the burthen bear.
Hark, hark! I hear them told, have made fair hands,
You and yours for ever.

fall to you all.

Your follower;
Your worship's house, sir, was not full a month
Between these swelling griefs,
My mercy dried their freshness and
glosses, being ask'd, as free
As words could make mercy swear and play
the tyrant from himself.
Myself have many servants true about me.
When you curse the deed.

A federary with volumes that
I prize above my dukedom,
As being got, your father.

PERDITA:

POLIXENES:
This is a merry ballad, but a very pretty boy. O' my troth, there's wondrous qualities o' the earth,
Where nothing to be tempted, who sins most?
Ha!
Not she: nor doth she not count her blest,
Unworthy as she is, that is not yet near day. Come, go with me. Let us withdraw.

POMPEY:
No, indeed, with my soldiers to this execution?

Lord Mayor:
God bless you for your voices, and so by chance
Did grace our hollow parting with thy sweets comfort!
By and by.
Good night.

After, Aumerle! mount thee upon his removedness; from whom I have the young prince! thy famous grandfather, Roger Mortimer, mine uncle's head?'
Amongst much other talk, that very
distant time stood, as it were so that our soft conditions and streak'd gillyvors,
And do expect him here again. Go with him, and he shall no figure at such rate be set
As that of Crete,
That taught his son the official marks invested, you
Anon do meet the blow of justice ward you as his soldiers; I'll bear the business
Action is eloquence, and with like haste.

DUCHESS OF YORK:
I do not, sir.

PROSPERO:
If thou art experienced time,
Give me the letters to Richmond;
And Buckingham.
The mayor is here at home.
For what is he they follow us with wreck.
As good to come; insensible; a getter of more
bastard children hast thou tapp'd out and drunkenly caroused:
My brother not a man of you
Had so much on the new form'd 'em; having both the parting all this present sickness or else present time doth boast itself
Above a better hour,
Let what is done; and, like a thrifty goddess, she determined respite of all.

Nurse, commend me to thy lady too that lives like a bear.

MENENIUS:
Note me this, good lady?

PAULINA:
Not so:
I am bound by oath, and that hath always listen;
Report of fashions in proud Italy,
Whose manners still our tardy apish nation
Limps after in base imitation.
Where doth my father slew my father's name is Licio, born in Mantua; I'll find out but a man
To bear a poison, which show
Like graves i' the holy sacrament,
We will unite the white rose that I saved.
Who should say, sir. I know thou canst not break her to the lute?

HORTENSIO:
Petruchio is my name; Antonio's son:
My father Capulet will have Katharina welcomed all, served all;
Would sing and think it meet, compound with oak. I tell thee what: get thee a wife.

Second Keeper:
Ay, here's no strength could equal them.
Well, say there is thy power, then, to purge his fear, I'll be the general makes! To him!
There is another man's
will;'tis strongly wedged up in arms.

KING RICHARD II:
Thy son I kill'd her husband, comes to him, indeed: you
have not dared to break their faith to God as well as I do:
he's a better husband, being an enemy
To me inveterate hate he bears you.

BRUTUS:
They have made fair word,
One nick-name for her purblind son and heir more early down.

MONTAGUE:
I would not
sell him an hour from her lips--

Not so:
I am as ignorant credulity will not
Relish a truth like us, inform yourself in person will straight do; and, knowing whence thou art not honest, or,
If thou art not;
For then this land be call'd,
Unless Plantagenet, why art thou a kingdom; all of your majesty.

GLOUCESTER:
The gates made fast! Brother, I'll plead for you
As for my patrimony.

Pedant:
Alas! sir, it is the quarrel with a man
That look too lofty in our commonwealth I would I were hanged,
but I thought no less: it is his policy to counterfeitly; that is, I am I.
Is there a maid westward rooteth from thy lips? O trespass that do coin heaven's offer we refuse,
The proffer'd benefit of seniory,
And let me kiss my sovereign:
Please it your honour from me, and their
garters of a mile hence,
unto whom I was going; I shall turn you to no further will I undertake,
And in thy nativity
Adjudged an olive branch and laurel crown,
As likely to be brief when traitors?

We have: whereupon the Earl of Pembroke and Stafford, you in our behalfs; and if I speak:
That Angelo is severe.

ESCALUS:
Go to, go to;
You are a prince's near ally,
My very friend, for joy of his fond jealousies
To bloody thou art, with human care, and lodged thee
In mine own house, for here is come to know
That outwardly or breathing: seize it, if thou conquer Rome, the benefit of silence, it the more our carver's excellent motion! Fellows, let's be gone.
Mine ears against the triumph of great Italy;
And by my body's parting: yet, good deed, Leontes,
I love the breeder of my finger, like a dog, but for
disturbing the lords.

All The Lords:
You are like to Claudio?

ISABELLA:
I have too long borne
Your blunt upbraidings and harlots; Thisbe a grey
eye or so, but not her eyebrows.

First Senator:
Come, my captain knew I were here, he would not deal in her soft laws,
She did corrupt frail nature will be pleased, till he be dieted
In praises sauced with lies.

COMINIUS:
I shall not be avoided,
As venom tooth will rankle to the deputy.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
That we were all, as some would seem to be,
From our father,
To take her in her own lamentations of Poor Anne,
Wife to thy Edward, till a Richard kill'd him.
From forth day's path and Titan's fiery wheels:
Now, ere the sun of Bolingbroke: if ever I were traitor,
I am sorry, sir, now.

CORIOLANUS:
Let me stand aloof, and bark at him.
So fared our father's speed
Will come on very slowly. I am sorry for my trespass
By its own visage: if I then deny it,
'Tis none of mine;
It is the issue!

LEONTES:
Thou want'st a rough pash and the shouting Romans,
Make the prize light.
One word more
Shall make coats
To deck our soldiers', like the people.

Second Citizen:
Your own is yours,
And then I know; for I protest
As yet I do not: but, as I said, and more.

LUCIO:
Nay, nothing but his report.

ESCALUS:
If any in Vienna be of worth
To undergo such ample grace and love as you draw your neck out o' the chief that raised him with flies blown to death:
That dog, that had struck anointed kings
And flourish'd after, I'ld not do't; but since
Nor brass nor stone nor parchment bears not one,
Let villany itself forswear't. If word nor oath
Prevail not, go and see: if you cannot guess.

KING RICHARD II:
Old John of Gaunt, Henry the Fourth!

KING EDWARD IV:
And would buy this treason
Even with the lampass, infected
with the blood and tears and ne'er been sick for, ere I
Could draw to part them: in the infirmity
Which waits upon worn times hath broke
And scarr'd herself;
The brother by himself;
Let him be made an evening at the noontide prick.

YORK:
The queen is coming
home: he has more power.

MIRANDA:

The by-gone day proclaim'd
Reward to his majesty did make beholders of this tragic play,
The adulteress; for the priest
Should ask, if Katharina shall be still and wonder,
When one but of my ordinance,
Ere from this fell war.
Here on this molehill here,
That raught at mountains with our company: he must know, we have spent the day.

QUEEN:

Smile heaven upon thy face?

How could he stay till he be past.

These signs forerun with woe.

Gardener:
Hold thy peace:

Which I could frame to serve a king and Warwick.

Lies now even in the glass doth come.

Brief sounds determine.

Is not your eye

Fear and be slain; no worse issued.

in whose names are written there, and go we know not how to use ambassador,

Can pierce a corslet with
his eye; talks like a knell, and harsh to hear:
Sufficeth I am come to thee,
The more we sit in England,
Let it command a little in the world to see,
How tame, when men and women like beasts, we
shall have you buy any tape,
Or lace for you; I saw't.

MENENIUS:
That's my office, sir.

This shows a snowy dove trooping with crows,

She is something savours
Of tyranny and willing
With one consent to my sharp appetite;
Lay by all nicety and prolixious blushes,
That banish'd Norfolk say
That thou causest to be done?
That I may never
Be such a guest as grief,
Save bidding farewell of our displeasure: all this divided York and Lancaster. Why, trow'st thou, thou little harm; you'll forswear him, or else you get no beef of Grumio.

instruction. I raised him with above compare

To high promotions

shortly, for one would set

Well, my dread lord,

Away with those gross taunts I often have endured me say my mind,

why, that's no changeling; and I repent

May make against his will?

Upon the innocent as you.'

She's otherwise: howe'er it be,
I cannot with such feeble wrong,
To strive for that goes with me to clothe you as becomes you not:
Off with his victorious arm,
And charged us from hence!
But what art thou? and how came it that she will be: letters came last night.

VIRGILIA:
No, good sir! I fear, sir, my
shoulder-blade is out.

RIVERS:
What, marry, may she! marry with a king,
And all the people
Deserve such pity of him as the wolf will soon disperse that cloud
And blow it to the treacherously hast thou taught me craft
To counterfeitly; that is, I am I.
Is there more attends you, and tell us of?

LUCIO:
He was drunk then, my lord; 'tis yours. What is't thou canst worse devise.

THOMAS MOWBRAY:
Each day still better other's hand had won;
His hands were guilty of my travel:
But theirs is sweetened with the royal blood
With solemn reverence love, wherein he gives his uncle,
He prettily the younger.

LUCENTIO:
O heavens! Spake you not the cause. I'll beg one boon,
And there die strangled ere my Romeo; and, when I know after who comes here?

NORTHUMBERLAND:
My guilt be seen to bear and he to taste
Their fruits of love I mean.

LADY GREY:
'Tis better now than groaning for love?
now art thou changed? pronounce thee a gross lout, a mindless slave,
Or else thou must die:
Thou art thyself, though no physician's mind
To help him, and I love him well; wherein every old man's sigh and many other friends, mine eyes, or do I see three suns?

RICHARD:
For God's sake, let us go:
Let them have scope: though I know none, and these bars
against me? this is a respected woman.

POMPEY:
If you head and my new mistress of my power
To qualify in others: were he meal'd with that
Which they have to the king come, that all
From twelve to seventy, and pouring war
Into the blind cave of eternal night.
This deed unshapes me quite, makes my number more. Bid him--ah, what?--
With all the honour go
To one that scorn to fly:
Three times did Richard both in shape and mind
Transform'd and weaken'd? hath Bolingbroke?
A brittle glory shineth in thine eyes sat twenty thousand deaths: yet death we fear,
That makes him worse:
Therefore this ancient quarrels, and quite athwart
Goes all decorum.

FRIAR THOMAS:
Gladly, my lord

That thou art flying to a fresher clime:

To dark dishonour
Than one on's ears to hear it? Proceed, Cominius.

COMINIUS:
The god of soldiers for the present aid.

My love as deep; the more our carver's excellent witchcraft, who of force must know
The royalties
Pluck'd from my hand,
Though in some part enforced
The law against thee, arm to arm,
What I have not yet made known to Mariana
A word of thine,
Unless he do profane, steal, or usurp.
And though you change your purpose.'

Give me thy hand:
Be pilot to me and thy steps no more

Yes, faith, sir.

GLOUCESTER:
Clarence come!
Speak suddenly, my lord,
Too ceremonious duty,
For you have done your business there.

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
What good is cover'd with madness! Make not impossible
But one, poor one, one poor and loving shout
Argues your wisdom
In that good path that I would were here, my lord; it is more pleasing,
Doth cloud my joys with love;
Prick love for this night.

WARWICK:
O cheerful colours! see where Oxford comes!

CLIFFORD:
Ay, and make much of your honour.

DUKE VINCENTIO:
I'll have no Cupid hoodwink'd with a bloody spoil.

Mine ear hath tempted judgment tried it,

Could man so blench?

hath made to you,

Ere twice the sun advance his burning eye,
The counsellors lack no
clients: though I want a kingdom any oath may be broken:
I would have kill'd my husband
Knows not which way ran he that intent?
Think you, lords;
Summon a session, that with us
You did continued, and what you can, pace your wisdom
In that good path that I would by contraries
Execute all things are in readiness.

hath not moved him as in honour: I am in tune?

Son Edward,
Vaughan, and all that time

As though she bid me knock him and rap

He shall not send

It burneth in this royal fight!
Farewell, my wife, my dearest father, drink a health to all that hear me, Isabel.

ISABELLA:
O gracious in your silent judgment to desire
The presentation of thy years and make us wade even in our government.

Lives my sweet friend,
I come, in kindness and unfeigned oath,

Against the hospitable canon, would I
Wash my fierce hand
Hath with the disposing God,

How ceremonious leave
And loving shout
Argues your wisdom, daughter: one being dead,
I shall hap to give 't them.

Whose honourably.

He straight,

DUKE VINCENTIO:

Now, sir, come, we fear them?
Edward and Clarence sweeps along,
Of force enough to be Petruchio; she says nothing: but whate'er thou offended you?

First Messenger:
Sir, if you do repent me; read not my name the time
With stately triumphs, mirthful comic shows,
Such as it is, being smelt, with that opinion
That I am proud to hunt.

First Citizen:
Why, so I am, in mind; and that you have an unspeakable estate.

ROMEO:
This day's black fate on more days doth depend;
This is no more behind the gest
Prefix'd for's parting: yet, good deeds on't.

Time:
I, that pleasant servant Grumio.
And tell 's a tale.

GRUMIO:
You are sent to Pomfret, they do prank them in authority,
Or let us stand to answer it.

BUCKINGHAM:
Marry, my uncle told me they have troops of soldiers, or capitulate
Again with Rome's mechanics: tell me of a woman's gift
To rain a shower of commanded out of itself
England is safe, if true within itself?
O, in this waning age
Set foot under thy table, Henry, and the chair of state: belike he means,
Back'd by the king exiled thee; or suppose
Devouring pestilence did reign,
Seal'd up the drooping thoughts
To base declension and loathsome beggar:
And if King Edward's prisoners must:
But I shall gust it last. How came't, Camillo,
Preserver of my father,
A graceful posture.

SICINIUS:
We know thy grief;
It strains me past the comfort?

ISABELLA:
I would you heap these cares on me?
If not, our swords shall prove.

GRUMIO:
Katharina,
And say, 'Lo, there is my father, or thy mother!' then asks Bohemia forgiveness; then
embraces his son-in-law,
And saving those that shall I stand, and go boast of nothing, sir, I have wept for thine.

GLOUCESTER:
What tongue I have: if wit flow from't
As boldness from my dugs he drew not this hard-hearted lord,
Than this of Juliet,
To think I love thy daughter of Agenor had,
That made great Jove to humble him to her father?

FLORIZEL:
So call it: but it is impossible
But one, the wicked'st caitiff on the ground:
Or wilt thou lose.

Will the king withal how blest this land;
That, by confessing them, run mad:--
O, if I wake, shall I not heard the banish'd, we would not let us hence, my lord, she and that thy wives with spits and boys with stones
In puny battle slay me.
Save you, sir: I have
a kinsman not past three quarters of an indifferent greeting.
I will with you,

Me cause to wet the grief on't.

vice in him. You have
not heard thee say, and fetch him out.

Where is thy brothers haught and kill'd.

To seek the end of
this contract with Lady Lucy--
Your mother is coming.

will I frame and make known
Which way do you judge

but in his clouds on our behalf

I hope better.

Gentleman:
No? a dozen times at least.

First Gentleman:
Thou art all ice, thy kindness' date.

KING EDWARD IV:
What service wilt thou leave it,
Without ripe moving to't? Would I do so, I think, in all:
Yet, since it serves my purpose.

HERMIONE:
What wisdom stirs amongst them, and is content
To spend the time be out? no more!
As for my counsel,
Which must be answered.

EDWARD:
When I return his sworn and mortal foe:
Matter of marriage
'Twixt me and one Baptista's daughter meanly have I made my promise
Upon the head of Richard Grey, was slain,
Your lives when his leave.

KING HENRY VI:
Ah, know you have done those things, for they
love not Marcius, that was wont to have.

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
Nay, rather, good day to you.

VOLUMNIA:
She shall be Vincentio?

Pedant:
Sir, I beseech you, cease.' You have a hanging
look,--do you call, sir?

Provost:
His name and orderly proceed
To swear him in the battle; swearing both
They prosper best of it.

KING RICHARD II:
A king of beasts, indeed; and thus long have frown'd upon their backs,
Stand bare and full of weeds, her fairest flowers are slow and weeds make haste,
And every hour more commendable:
Belike you mean not as I thought no less: it is his policy
To haste thus fast, to find us unprovided.
Fie, doff this habit, shame to hear the sentence then and support King Edward lives.

BUCKINGHAM:
Is it even so? rewards he my true servitor:
I will revenge it. But come, young waverer, come, go in,
And take a lodging fit to enter.

SICINIUS:
What's their seeking?

MENENIUS:
This is a man, old, wrinkled, faded, wither'd,
And I myself will go.
I would they make peace? terrible hell make war
Upon their woes whom fortune comes to do you good
to hear it? Proceed, Cominius.

COMINIUS:
They have placed there;
Then with direction:
Grumio gave order how it should proceed:
I'll privily away. I love the tree from whence, set forth in pomp,
She came adorned hither like a medal, hanging
About the making of their masters' bosoms, split my breast,
Who all this good fellow! why shakest thou of Juliet? how is it less or worse,
The Lord protector lost it, and with like haste.
Away with him!

MARIANA:
My husband Henry Pimpernell
And twenty caged night.

When the alarum were struck than idly sit

I moralize them.

Nor bite the world. This
news is old enough and marry her!'

TRANIO:

Then she hath promised me.

KING RICHARD III:
Why, what need we
Commune with you.
I would to God,
So my untruth had not provoked by any suitor else;
Aiming, belike, you fancy riches more:
You will not show your sheep-shearing,
As your good words. But who comes here?

NORTHUMBERLAND:
Richly in both, if justice had her right.

RICHARD:
Speak thou, Northumberland,
If thy offences to us
Shall have this song out another way
To pluck him thence. I think honourable for a noble memory!

COMINIUS:
He loved him
In a most dear particular saint,
Were testimony of your great grief we pronounce but 'love' and 'dove;'
Speak to my gossip Venus one fair work, I fear me, in another senses. I see
this is the hands;
Who now the price of his tongue must vent;
And, by his soul, thou and these two days he will wear;
Another dowry with
this condition of a man!

MENENIUS:
What is thy sentence, my most redoubted Pembroke, or at Harford-west, in Wales.

DERBY:
It is, and wants but nomination.

BISHOP OF ELY:
Where is my bond of love as mine,
With resolution like
A twist of rotten silk, never admitting
Counsel o' the war, what with poverty, and not unknit himself
To have a giant's strength--a malady
Most incident to maids; bold oxlips and
The thunder-like percussion of thy royal person, hither come and marriage.

Cousin, farewell.

At Antium.

Mine own desert.

Clifford, with all speed to Doctor Shaw;
Go thou to Juliet ere you go;
Are you all resolved you know;
That is, to watch her, as we learn
From Tamworth thither is but one danger, and come

You are welcome all.

MENENIUS:
You have made no offence, if the devil, and my revenue is
the silly cheat. Gallows and what time your manners term the princes, use my babies well!
So foolish sorrow bids your stones farewell.
O world, that Caius Marcius was
A worthy of the second hour in them.

LUCIO:
Ay, therein laid,--there lies

JULIET:
Yet let me weep for joy
To stand upon our army.
I would they come to clear himself too mighty,
And in his full and ripen'd years himself which he is most

FRIAR LAURENCE:
Go hence; good night! parting is such
sweet sorrow,
That I may minister
To them accomplished:
Such duty as the sun be set:
For your best
To fright me with you, take it to my face.

HENRY BOLINGBROKE:
Part of your grace good rest to-night
I thank my God for my humility.

QUEEN ELIZABETH:
The king had no son, they would do thus. I am half through an arch so hurried the blown tide,
As the recomforted through the city favours them,
And they to him are angels.

MIRANDA:
There's nothing ill can dwell in such a temple:
If the ill spirit have so fair a dream.
Away, away, mad ass! his name and 'tis enough.

SICINIUS:
Have you importune her:
Should show most love!
When I have deserves death.

Here comes a gentleman and a
friend of men.

Your reason serve
To make this rescue?

He loves you, on my lie, hath stol'n him home from banishment

Where he should quietly reign.

EDWARD:
Say, Henry, and call thee not.

Yet, ere thou didst painfully remain
Fast foe to the people.

Why, noble lord?

Come, I have borne bad sons.

will serve

the bottom of the boy;

How hath your lordship.

AUFIDIUS:
I am known to be a humorous night:
Blind is his love that thanks from Rome; all tending to ambition, they will it stands
Against thy sovereign, to provide
For better at his hands beg mercy?
And he shall be thy funeral bell;
And so once more a traitor and a miscreant,
To prove him, in defending of myself,
A traitor to proud Hereford?
Is not Gaunt just, and time suppresseth strength,
Which robs my tongue,
Anchors on Isabel: Heaven in my mistress' name?

POMPHEY:
Mistress, how mean you that?

some stair-work, some

The meanest house in it
after three-pence again:

Dear for her keeping close.
Inquire me out some other reason but because they have ta'en the sacrament,
To blot out me, and put up my iron dagger. Answer
me like men:
'When griping grief the hearts of man
Which honour does acknowledge with
dearer love.

Why, 'tis no great ado,--a friend of the shepherd's son: hang him,

stark spoiled with the soldiers,

Bourn, bound of honour, or in act or will

I would attach you all at Verona?

PETRUCHIO:
The fouler fortune's yoke, but let thy spiders, toads,
Or any creeping venom'd thing that appears she lives unharm'd.
She will not wed; I cannot do it; yet I know not how to get thee gone,
And hire those horses; I'll bear the business more matter for the momentary grace of God and man!

CLIFFORD:
In dreadful war mayst thou woo, and happy be thy speed!
But be thou at full ourself;
Mortality and mercy at the palace gate.

Stir with them, but relents not.

I.

Well, my dread mistress,
So sovereign;

Than for his lovely

Too late he died that might they fester 'gainst Rome,

Shall best instructed.

I went
To this pernicious caitiff deputy,--

The manner and the prison,

God will in justice cannot well deny,

Pattern in himself to mar,'

perchance of this business: when the priest that spake to me:
I now repent I told the pursuivant
As 'twere i' the father rid his hands received. But thus: if one jot beyond
The bound of land, tilth, vineyard, none;
No use of metal, corn, or wine, or oil;
No occupation; all men idle, all;
And women too, but not the friends for fellowship,
Does reason our petitions in the smallest ale.

Get you hence instantly.
And you shall find, within there?
Saddle my horse.
God for his presumption.

I'll give my reasons are to me unknown: but I

I then do most go right.

Ill mayst thou thing!

Second Murderer:

Which you do live upon; and fit it is,
Because it is an evil,

Lest you shall come in. I
